4c:["$","p",null,{"style":{"fontSize":"1rem","color":"var(--text-body)","lineHeight":1.75,"marginBottom":"1.25em","marginTop":0},"children":[["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"Tile coding"}],": partition the continuous state space into overlapping grids. Each tile\nis a region of state space; the feature vector has a 1 in the component corresponding to\neach tile the current state falls into, and 0 elsewhere. But understanding the linear case first is essential: it isolates the approximation error from the optimization error.
